## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    SA[ServiceAccount: argocd-backup-tool]
    CRB[ClusterRoleBinding: argocd-backup-binding]
    CR[ClusterRole: argocd-backup-role]
    Resources[Resources: pods, configmaps, secrets, argoproj.io/*]
    
    SA --> CRB
    CR --> CRB
    CRB --> Resources
    CR -.permissions.-> Resources
    
    subgraph Permissions
        P1[get, list, watch pods]
        P2[get, list, watch configmaps]
        P3[get, list, watch secrets]
        P4[get, list, watch argoproj.io/*]
    end
    
    Resources --> Permissions
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Helm
    participant Namespace
    participant ServiceAccount
    participant ClusterRole
    participant ClusterRoleBinding
    participant CronJob
    participant Job
    
    Helm->>Namespace: Create namespace
    Helm->>ServiceAccount: Create service account (conditional)
    Helm->>ClusterRole: Create cluster role
    Helm->>ClusterRoleBinding: Bind SA to ClusterRole
    Helm->>CronJob: Create scheduled backup job
    Helm->>Job: Create post-install/upgrade job
    Job->>Job: Execute backup immediately
    CronJob->>CronJob: Execute on schedule
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Install
    Install --> CreateNamespace
    CreateNamespace --> CreateServiceAccount
    CreateServiceAccount --> CreateClusterRole
    CreateClusterRole --> CreateClusterRoleBinding
    CreateClusterRoleBinding --> CreateCronJob
    CreateCronJob --> CreateJob
    CreateJob --> PostInstallBackup
    PostInstallBackup --> Running
    Running --> ScheduledBackup
    ScheduledBackup --> Running
    Running --> Upgrade
    Upgrade --> PostUpgradeBackup
    PostUpgradeBackup --> Running
```
